 ) aaj pakistan se bharat aae kareeb 450 hindu pariwaron par apni sahyogi aditi rajput kii ek khaas report dekh rahaa tha, jo is samay dilli ke antarraji bas adde ke kareeb majanuun kaa tila main sharan liye hue hai
 Tired of discrimination in Pakistan, these people have come to India, and want to stay here, but they have neither job, nor accommodation
 yahaan tak ki sirf dilli kaa visa he, isliye dilli se baahar bhi nahin ja sakate
 By the way, these people have requested Prime Minister Narendra Modi for help, and Home Minister Rajnath Singh is going to have a meeting with 10 organizations on 23 December to solve their problems quickly
 yah kahani sirf in hindu pariwaron tak hi simit nahin he, kyonki pakistan se palaayan kar bharat aae hinduon kii sankhya lakhon main he
 When India was partitioned in the year 1947, millions of Hindus and Muslims changed the country on the basis of religion
 phir bhi kuch musalmaan aise the, jo bharat main hi rah gaye, or isi tarah kuch hindu pakistan main
 India preferred to become a secular state instead of becoming a Hindu nation, so that minorities living in India do not consider themselves insecure, they get equal rights and for this, India has included freedom to choose religion in the list of fundamental rights in its constitution
 
 bharat vibhaajan se pehle musalamaanon kii sankhya bharat kii kul aabaadi kaa 10 pratishat thi, jo aaj badhkar lagbhag 15 pratishat ho gai he
 But the fate of Hindus living in Pakistan was not like Indian Muslims then, nor is it today
 pakistan main based hinduon main se lagbhag 96 fisadi sindh praant main hi rahete hai
 The constitution of Pakistan was formed in the year 1956 and Pakistan became an Islamic country, abandoning progressive and liberal ideologies, and since then Hindus have become living there
 pakistan jab bhi bharat ke aage munh kii khaataa, yaa bharat main sampradayik dange hote, sabhi ghatnaon kaa dushprinaam pakistan main rahane vaale hinduon ko bhugatna padataa
 Whether it was the indo-pak war, or the demolition of the disputed structure in Ayodhya, or the riots in Gujarat, the Hindus of Pakistan were targeted by the government and people of their anger
 bharat main 6 disambar, 1992 ko ayodhya main vivaadit dhaancha giraae jane se pakistan main hinduon ke khilaaf tikhi pratikriyaayein huin
 According to Minority Right Group International, about 120 Hindu temples were demolished in Pakistan during 2–8 December 1992
 zia-ul-haq kii taanaashaahee se lekar ab taliban ke atyaacharon tak pakistani hinduon kaa jivan dubhar hi rahaa he
 There were a total of 428 temples in Pakistan at the time of independence, of which now only 26 remain
 pakistan main zyaadaatar hindu mandir yaa gira die gaye, yaa unhen hotel bana diya gaya he
 According to the 2012 report of Pakistan's National Commission for Justice and Peace, 74 percent of Hindu women are sexually abused
 pakistan ke maanavadhikaar ayog kii varsh 2012 kii report ke mutabik pakistan ke sindh praant main har maheene 20 se 25 hindu ladakiyon kaa apharan hota he or jabardastee dharm parivartan karaayaa jaataa he
 When there is no favorable conditions for living in Pakistan, then Hindus are forced to leave Pakistan in large numbers
 pakistan kii janaganana (1951) ke mutabik pakistan kii kul aabaadi main 22 fisadi hindu the, jo 1998 kii janaganana main ghatakar 1
 6 percent are left
 human ritis lau network kii ek report ke mutabik varsh 1965 se lekar ab tak takreeban sava lakh pakistani hinduon ne bharat kii taraf palaayan kiya he
 By the way, when Muslims are not safe in Pakistan, where to complain for Hindus
 
 
 ? vahaan mandiron main hi nahin, masjidon main bhi dhamaake hote rahete hai

 kisi party kaa vot bank nahin ban pate
